<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sample_translation">Sample translation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Li_Bai&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Sample translation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%8B%E7%8D%A8%E9%85%8C%E4%B8%80.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="240" data-file-width="797" decoding="async" height="66" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%8B%E7%8D%A8%E9%85%8C%E4%B8%80.svg/220px-%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%8B%E7%8D%A8%E9%85%8C%E4%B8%80.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%8B%E7%8D%A8%E9%85%8C%E4%B8%80.svg/330px-%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%8B%E7%8D%A8%E9%85%8C%E4%B8%80.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%8B%E7%8D%A8%E9%85%8C%E4%B8%80.svg/440px-%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%8B%E7%8D%A8%E9%85%8C%E4%B8%80.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%8B%E7%8D%A8%E9%85%8C%E4%B8%80.svg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Text of Li Bai's poem "Drinking Alone by Moonlight", in the classical top-to-bottom, right-to-left order</div></div></div>
<p>One of Li Bai's best known poems and a good example of his writing is his <i>Drinking Alone by Moonlight</i> (<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">月下獨酌</span></span>, <i>Yuèxià Dúzhuó</i>), which has been translated into English by various authors, including this translation, by <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Waley" title="Arthur Waley">Arthur Waley</a>:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[65]</a></sup>
</p>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r996844942" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><blockquote class="templatequote"><div class="poem">
<p><span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">花間一壺酒。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>A cup of wine, under the flowering trees;<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">獨酌無相親。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>I drink alone, for no friend is near.<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">舉杯邀明月。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>Raising my cup I beckon the bright moon,<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">對影成三人。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>For he, with my shadow, will make three men.<br/>
<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">月既不解飲。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>The moon, alas, is no drinker of wine;<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">影徒隨我身。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>Listless, my shadow creeps about at my side.<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">暫伴月將影。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>Yet with the moon as friend and the shadow as slave<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">行樂須及春。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>I must make merry before the Spring is spent.<br/>
<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">我歌月徘徊。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>To the songs I sing the moon flickers her beams;<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">我舞影零亂。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>In the dance I weave my shadow tangles and breaks.<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">醒時同交歡。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>While we were sober, three shared the fun;<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">醉後各分散。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>Now we are drunk, each goes his way.<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">永結無情遊。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>May we long share our odd, inanimate feast,<br/>
<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">相期邈雲漢。</span></span><span class="nowrap">   </span>And meet at last on the Cloudy River of the sky.
</p>
</div></blockquote>
<div class="thumb tnone" style="margin-left:auto;margin-right:auto;overflow:hidden;width:auto;max-width:3008px"><div class="thumbinner"><div class="noresize" style="overflow:auto;direction:rtl"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Li_Bai_calligraphy_of_Shang_Yang_Tie,_Tang_dynasty.jpg" title='‪The calligraphy "Shang Yang Tie" (上陽貼) by Li Bai.‬'><img alt="" data-file-height="640" data-file-width="5676" decoding="async" height="338" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Li_Bai_calligraphy_of_Shang_Yang_Tie%2C_Tang_dynasty.jpg/3000px-Li_Bai_calligraphy_of_Shang_Yang_Tie%2C_Tang_dynasty.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Li_Bai_calligraphy_of_Shang_Yang_Tie%2C_Tang_dynasty.jpg/4500px-Li_Bai_calligraphy_of_Shang_Yang_Tie%2C_Tang_dynasty.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3a/Li_Bai_calligraphy_of_Shang_Yang_Tie%2C_Tang_dynasty.jpg 2x" width="3000"/></a></div><div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Li_Bai_calligraphy_of_Shang_Yang_Tie,_Tang_dynasty.jpg" title="File:Li Bai calligraphy of Shang Yang Tie, Tang dynasty.jpg"> </a></div>The calligraphy "Shang Yang Tie" (<span title="Chinese-language text"><span lang="zh-Hant">上陽貼</span></span>) by Li Bai.</div></div></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_popular_culture">In popular culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Li_Bai&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: In popular culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Portrayed by Wong Wai-leung in the 2000 television series <i><a href="/wiki/The_Legend_of_Lady_Yang" title="The Legend of Lady Yang">The Legend of Lady Yang</a></i></li>
<li>An actor playing Li Bai narrates the <a href="/wiki/Wonders_of_China" title="Wonders of China">Wonders of China</a> and <a href="/wiki/Reflections_of_China" title="Reflections of China">Reflections of China</a> films at the <a href="/wiki/China_Pavilion_at_Epcot" title="China Pavilion at Epcot">China Pavilion at Epcot</a></li>
<li>Li Bai's poem 'Hard Roads in Shu' is sung by a Chinese singer AnAn in a Liu Bei trailer for a game <a href="/wiki/Total_War:_Three_Kingdoms" title="Total War: Three Kingdoms">Total War: Three Kingdoms</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup></li>
<li>He appears as a "great writer" in the game <a href="/wiki/Civilization_VI" title="Civilization VI">Civilization VI</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup></li></ul>

Li Bai wrote 4 poems with the same name (<i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quantangshi" title="Quantangshi">Quantangshi</a></i> 卷182_22 《月下獨酌四首》李白); Waley published translations of three.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-66"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-66">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation cs2"><a class="external text" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4UhSsPhIpqM" rel="nofollow"><i>Total War: THREE KINGDOMS - Liu Bei Launch Trailer</i></a><span class="reference-accessdate">, retrieved <span class="nowrap">28 August</span> 2022</span></cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Total+War%3A+THREE+KINGDOMS+-+Liu+Bei+Launch+Trailer&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3D4UhSsPhIpqM&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALi+Bai"></span></span>
</li>
